COVID-2019 in UA

Sergiy = Chornyy
In = this research used prediction models based on pandemic equations by William Og= ilvy Kermack and  A. G. McKendrick (https://doi.org/10.1098/rspa.1927.0118).
Thei= r model adopted to official COVID-2019 statistics from Ukrainian Ministry of Heal= th.
Exp= ected epidemic peak is its 44-th day (4/28/2020) and expected end of the epidem= ia is its 100-th day (6/23/2020). 
Expe= cted maximum of registered  infected people by= this model  is  62590 persons. 
Per= iod when daily registered infected people will be more 1000 is 4/17/2020-5/12/2020 with maximum about 2505 per day summary for Ukraine.
 Model will be dynamically changed in accordance to new statistics data.
Gra= phs above are the results of autor's own scientific research, reflects his point of view and are not official data of any Governmental  institutions of Ukraine.
